mysql> SELECT p.productname, YEAR(t.transactiondate) AS year, MONTH(t.transactiondate) AS month, SUM(t.totalvalue) AS monthly_sales
    -> FROM Products p
    -> JOIN Transactions t ON p.productid = t.productid
    -> GROUP BY p.productname, YEAR(t.transactiondate), MONTH(t.transactiondate)
    -> HAVING p.productid IN (
    ->     SELECT productid FROM (
    ->         SELECT productid, SUM(quantity) AS total_units
    ->         FROM Transactions
    ->         GROUP BY productid
    ->         ORDER BY total_units DESC
    ->         LIMIT 3
    ->     ) AS TopProducts
    -> )
    -> ORDER BY p.productname, year, month;
ERROR 1054 (42S22): Unknown column 'p.productid' in 'IN/ALL/ANY subquery'
